I have always had a good experience staying at InterContinental hotels, and I am an IHG member. From now on, I will never stay at a Crown hotel again! And this hotel is really average, the location is very remote, the room size is small, the restaurant staff are very good, but after staying for a few days, the tableware is very unclean! Especially the coffee cup in the western restaurant had stains on it, which were obviously not cleaned by the dishwasher.
